  45 | class CandidateValidationError(ValueError):
  46 |     """Raised when an evolved candidate violates the benchmark contract."""
  47 | 
  48 | 
  49 | def _load_metadata() -> dict[str, Any]:
  50 |     with TARGET_METADATA_PATH.open() as f:
  51 |         return json.load(f)
  52 | 
  53 | 
  54 | TARGET_METADATA = _load_metadata()
  55 | ALLOWED_HOTSPOTS = set(TARGET_METADATA["target"]["allowed_hotspots"])
  56 | INTERFACE_HOTSPOTS = [item["hotspot"] for item in TARGET_METADATA["interface_hotspot_candidates"]]
  57 | PRIOR_HOTSPOTS = TARGET_METADATA["prior_art_hotspots"]["hotspots"]
  58 | TARGET_PDB_PATH = ASSETS_DIR / TARGET_METADATA["target"]["target_pdb"]
  59 | 
  60 | 
  61 | def _is_module_docstring(node: ast.AST) -> bool:
  62 |     return isinstance(node, ast.Expr) and isinstance(node.value, ast.Constant) and isinstance(node.value.value, str)
  63 | 
  64 | 
  65 | def _is_main_guard(node: ast.AST) -> bool:
  66 |     if not isinstance(node, ast.If) or node.orelse:
  67 |         return False
  68 |     test = node.test
  69 |     if not isinstance(test, ast.Compare) or len(test.ops) != 1 or len(test.comparators) != 1:
  70 |         return False
  71 |     return (
  72 |         isinstance(test.left, ast.Name)
  73 |         and test.left.id == "__name__"
  74 |         and isinstance(test.ops[0], ast.Eq)
  75 |         and isinstance(test.comparators[0], ast.Constant)
  76 |         and test.comparators[0].value == "__main__"
  77 |     )
  78 | 
  79 | 
  80 | def _validate_candidate_source(program_path: str) -> None:
  81 |     source = Path(program_path).read_text()
  82 |     tree = ast.parse(source, filename=program_path)
  83 |     has_entrypoint = False
  84 | 
  85 |     for node in tree.body:
  86 |         if _is_module_docstring(node) or _is_main_guard(node):
  87 |             continue
  88 |         if isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):
  89 |             if node.module not in _ALLOWED_IMPORT_MODULES:
  90 |                 raise CandidateValidationError(f"import from {node.module!r} is not allowed")
  91 |             continue
  92 |         if isinstance(node, ast.Assign):
  93 |             try:
  94 |                 ast.literal_eval(node.value)
  95 |             except Exception as exc:
  96 |                 raise CandidateValidationError("top-level assignments must be literal constants") from exc
  97 |             continue
  98 |         if isinstance(node, ast.FunctionDef):
  99 |             if node.decorator_list:
 100 |                 raise CandidateValidationError("function decorators are not allowed")
 101 |             if node.name in {"propose_design_run", "run_discovery"}:
 102 |                 has_entrypoint = True
 103 |             for child in ast.walk(node):
 104 |                 if isinstance(child, (ast.Import, ast.ImportFrom)):
 105 |                     raise CandidateValidationError("imports inside evolved functions are not allowed")
 106 |                 if isinstance(child, ast.Call) and isinstance(child.func, ast.Name) and child.func.id in _FORBIDDEN_CALLS:
 107 |                     raise CandidateValidationError(f"call to {child.func.id}() is not allowed")
 108 |             continue
 109 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"top-level {type(node).__name__} is not allowed")
 110 | 
 111 |     if not has_entrypoint:
 112 |         raise CandidateValidationError("candidate must define propose_design_run() or run_discovery()")
 113 | 
 114 | 
 115 | def _load_candidate_spec(program_path: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 116 |     _validate_candidate_source(program_path)
 117 |     spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("binder_candidate", program_path)
 118 |     if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
 119 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"could not load candidate: {program_path}")
 120 |     module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
 121 |     spec.loader.exec_module(module)
 122 | 
 123 |     fn = getattr(module, "propose_design_run", None) or getattr(module, "run_discovery", None)
 124 |     if fn is None:
 125 |         raise CandidateValidationError("missing propose_design_run() or run_discovery()")
 126 |     result = fn()
 127 |     if not isinstance(result, dict):
 128 |         raise CandidateValidationError("candidate entry point must return a dict")
 129 |     return result
 130 | 
 131 | 
 132 | def _as_int(value: Any, name: str, low: int, high: int) -> int:
 133 |     if isinstance(value, bool):
 134 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be an integer")
 135 |     try:
 136 |         out = int(value)
 137 |     except Exception as exc:
 138 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be an integer") from exc
 139 |     if out < low or out > high:
 140 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be between {low} and {high}")
 141 |     return out
 142 | 
 143 | 
 144 | def _as_float(value: Any, name: str, low: float, high: float) -> float:
 145 |     try:
 146 |         out = float(value)
 147 |     except Exception as exc:
 148 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be a number") from exc
 149 |     if not math.isfinite(out) or out < low or out > high:
 150 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be finite and between {low} and {high}")
 151 |     return out
 152 | 
 153 | 
 154 | def _normalise_hotspots(value: Any) -> list[str]:
 155 |     if value is None:
 156 |         value = PRIOR_HOTSPOTS
 157 |     if not isinstance(value, (list, tuple)):
 158 |         raise CandidateValidationError("hotspot_residues must be a list")
 159 |     hotspots = []
 160 |     for item in value:
 161 |         if not isinstance(item, str):
 162 |             raise CandidateValidationError("hotspot residues must be strings like 'B84'")
 163 |         residue = item.strip().upper()
 164 |         if not re.fullmatch(r"B\d+[A-Z]?", residue):
 165 |             raise CandidateValidationError(f"invalid hotspot residue format: {item!r}")
 166 |         if residue not in ALLOWED_HOTSPOTS:
 167 |             raise CandidateValidationError(f"hotspot {residue!r} is not a modeled chain-B residue")
 168 |         if residue not in hotspots:
 169 |             hotspots.append(residue)
 170 |     if not 1 <= len(hotspots) <= 8:
 171 |         raise CandidateValidationError("choose between 1 and 8 hotspot residues")
 172 |     return hotspots
 173 | 
 174 | 
 175 | def _normalise_length_range(value: Any) -> list[int]:
 176 |     if not isinstance(value, (list, tuple)) or len(value) != 2:
 177 |         raise CandidateValidationError("binder_length must be [min_len, max_len]")
 178 |     low = _as_int(value[0], "binder_length[0]", 40, 220)
 179 |     high = _as_int(value[1], "binder_length[1]", 40, 220)
 180 |     if low > high:
 181 |         raise CandidateValidationError("binder_length minimum cannot exceed maximum")
 182 |     if high - low > 120:
 183 |         raise CandidateValidationError("binder_length range is too wide for this benchmark")
 184 |     return [low, high]
 185 | 
 186 | 
 187 | def _normalise_schedule(value: Any, name: str, allowed_modes: set[str]) -> dict[str, Any]:
 188 |     if value is None:
 189 |         value = {}
 190 |     if not isinstance(value, dict):
 191 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be a dict")
 192 |     mode = str(value.get("mode", "log" if "schedule" in name else "1/t"))
 193 |     if mode not in allowed_modes:
 194 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name}.mode {mode!r} is unsupported")
 195 |     return {"mode": mode, "p": _as_float(value.get("p", 1.0), f"{name}.p", 0.05, 8.0)}
 196 | 
 197 | 
 198 | def _normalise_spec(raw: dict[str, Any], *, stage: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 199 |     sampling = raw.get("sampling", {})
 200 |     if sampling is None:
 201 |         sampling = {}
 202 |     if not isinstance(sampling, dict):
 203 |         raise CandidateValidationError("sampling must be a dict")
 204 | 
 205 |     search = raw.get("search", {})
 206 |     if search is None:
 207 |         search = {}
 208 |     if not isinstance(search, dict):
 209 |         raise CandidateValidationError("search must be a dict")
 210 | 
 211 |     algorithm = str(search.get("algorithm", "best-of-n"))
 212 |     if algorithm not in _ALLOWED_SEARCH_ALGORITHMS:
 213 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"unsupported search algorithm: {algorithm!r}")
 214 | 
 215 |     nsteps = _as_int(raw.get("denoising_steps", 80), "denoising_steps", 10, 400)
 216 |     if stage == "stage1":
 217 |         nsteps = min(nsteps, _as_int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_STAGE1_NSTEPS", 20), "stage1_nsteps", 5, 80))
 218 |     else:
 219 |         nsteps = min(nsteps, _as_int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_MAX_NSTEPS", 120), "max_nsteps", 10, 400))
 220 | 
 221 |     stage2_batch_cap = _as_int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_STAGE2_BATCH_SIZE", 2), "stage2_batch_cap", 1, 8)
 222 |     stage2_length_cap = _as_int(
 223 |         os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_STAGE2_NUM_LENGTH_SAMPLES", 2),
 224 |         "stage2_length_cap",
 225 |         1,
 226 |         8,
 227 |     )
 228 |     stage2_replica_cap = _as_int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_STAGE2_REPLICAS", 2), "stage2_replica_cap", 1, 8)
 229 | 
 230 |     batch_size = _as_int(raw.get("batch_size", 2), "batch_size", 1, 8)
 231 |     num_length_samples = _as_int(raw.get("num_length_samples", 2), "num_length_samples", 1, 8)
 232 |     if stage == "stage1":
 233 |         batch_size = min(batch_size, 1)
 234 |         num_length_samples = min(num_length_samples, 1)
 235 |     else:
 236 |         batch_size = min(batch_size, stage2_batch_cap)
 237 |         num_length_samples = min(num_length_samples, stage2_length_cap)
 238 | 
 239 |     best_of_n = search.get("best_of_n", {}) if isinstance(search.get("best_of_n", {}), dict) else {}
 240 |     beam_search = search.get("beam_search", {}) if isinstance(search.get("beam_search", {}), dict) else {}
 241 |     fk_steering = search.get("fk_steering", {}) if isinstance(search.get("fk_steering", {}), dict) else {}
 242 |     mcts = search.get("mcts", {}) if isinstance(search.get("mcts", {}), dict) else {}
 243 | 
 244 |     spec = {
 245 |         "hotspot_residues": _normalise_hotspots(raw.get("hotspot_residues")),
 246 |         "binder_length": _normalise_length_range(raw.get("binder_length", [70, 110])),
 247 |         "checkpoint_selection": str(raw.get("checkpoint_selection", "complexa_default")),
 248 |         "denoising_steps": nsteps,
 249 |         "self_conditioning": bool(raw.get("self_conditioning", True)),
 250 |         "seed": _as_int(raw.get("seed", 7), "seed", 0, 2**31 - 1),
 251 |         "num_length_samples": num_length_samples,
 252 |         "batch_size": batch_size,
 253 |         "sampling": {
 254 |             "bb_ca_schedule": _normalise_schedule(
 255 |                 sampling.get("bb_ca_schedule", {"mode": "log", "p": 2.0}),
 256 |                 "bb_ca_schedule",
 257 |                 _ALLOWED_SCHEDULE_MODES,
 258 |             ),
 259 |             "local_latents_schedule": _normalise_schedule(
 260 |                 sampling.get("local_latents_schedule", {"mode": "power", "p": 2.0}),
 261 |                 "local_latents_schedule",
 262 |                 _ALLOWED_SCHEDULE_MODES,
 263 |             ),
 264 |             "bb_ca_noise": _normalise_schedule(
 265 |                 sampling.get("bb_ca_noise", {"mode": "1/t", "p": 1.0}),
 266 |                 "bb_ca_noise",
 267 |                 _ALLOWED_NOISE_MODES,
 268 |             ),
 269 |             "local_latents_noise": _normalise_schedule(
 270 |                 sampling.get("local_latents_noise", {"mode": "tan", "p": 1.0}),
 271 |                 "local_latents_noise",
 272 |                 _ALLOWED_NOISE_MODES,
 273 |             ),
 274 |             "bb_ca_sc_scale_noise": _as_float(sampling.get("bb_ca_sc_scale_noise", 0.1), "bb_ca_sc_scale_noise", 0.0, 2.0),
 275 |             "local_latents_sc_scale_noise": _as_float(
 276 |                 sampling.get("local_latents_sc_scale_noise", 0.1),
 277 |                 "local_latents_sc_scale_noise",
 278 |                 0.0,
 279 |                 2.0,
 280 |             ),
 281 |             "bb_ca_sc_scale_score": _as_float(sampling.get("bb_ca_sc_scale_score", 1.0), "bb_ca_sc_scale_score", 0.0, 5.0),
 282 |             "local_latents_sc_scale_score": _as_float(
 283 |                 sampling.get("local_latents_sc_scale_score", 1.0),
 284 |                 "local_latents_sc_scale_score",
 285 |                 0.0,
 286 |                 5.0,
 287 |             ),
 288 |         },
 289 |         "search": {
 290 |             "algorithm": algorithm,
 291 |             "best_of_n": {"replicas": _as_int(best_of_n.get("replicas", 2), "best_of_n.replicas", 1, 8)},
 292 |             "beam_search": {
 293 |                 "n_branch": _as_int(beam_search.get("n_branch", 2), "beam_search.n_branch", 1, 8),
 294 |                 "beam_width": _as_int(beam_search.get("beam_width", 2), "beam_search.beam_width", 1, 8),
 295 |             },
 296 |             "fk_steering": {
 297 |                 "n_branch": _as_int(fk_steering.get("n_branch", 2), "fk_steering.n_branch", 1, 8),
 298 |                 "beam_width": _as_int(fk_steering.get("beam_width", 2), "fk_steering.beam_width", 1, 8),
 299 |                 "temperature": _as_float(fk_steering.get("temperature", 0.1), "fk_steering.temperature", 0.0, 5.0),
 300 |             },
 301 |             "mcts": {
 302 |                 "n_simulations": _as_int(mcts.get("n_simulations", 4), "mcts.n_simulations", 1, 64),
 303 |                 "exploration_prob": _as_float(mcts.get("exploration_prob", 0.4), "mcts.exploration_prob", 0.0, 1.0),
 304 |                 "exploration_constant": _as_float(
 305 |                     mcts.get("exploration_constant", 1.0),
 306 |                     "mcts.exploration_constant",
 307 |                     0.0,
 308 |                     10.0,
 309 |                 ),
 310 |             },
 311 |         },
 312 |     }
 313 |     if stage == "stage1":
 314 |         spec["search"]["best_of_n"]["replicas"] = min(spec["search"]["best_of_n"]["replicas"], 1)
 315 |         spec["search"]["beam_search"]["n_branch"] = min(spec["search"]["beam_search"]["n_branch"], 1)
 316 |         spec["search"]["beam_search"]["beam_width"] = min(spec["search"]["beam_search"]["beam_width"], 1)
 317 |         spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["n_branch"] = min(spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["n_branch"], 1)
 318 |         spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["beam_width"] = min(spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["beam_width"], 1)
 319 |         spec["search"]["mcts"]["n_simulations"] = min(spec["search"]["mcts"]["n_simulations"], 2)
 320 |     else:
 321 |         spec["search"]["best_of_n"]["replicas"] = min(spec["search"]["best_of_n"]["replicas"], stage2_replica_cap)
 322 |         spec["search"]["beam_search"]["n_branch"] = min(spec["search"]["beam_search"]["n_branch"], stage2_replica_cap)
 323 |         spec["search"]["beam_search"]["beam_width"] = min(spec["search"]["beam_search"]["beam_width"], stage2_replica_cap)
 324 |         spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["n_branch"] = min(spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["n_branch"], stage2_replica_cap)
 325 |         spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["beam_width"] = min(spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["beam_width"], stage2_replica_cap)
 326 |     return spec
 327 | 
 328 | 
 329 | def _resolve_checkpoint(spec: dict[str, Any]) -> tuple[Path, str, Path]:
 330 |     ckpt_root = Path(os.environ.get("CKPT_PATH", str(PROTEINA_ROOT / "ckpts"))).expanduser()
 331 |     selection = spec["checkpoint_selection"]
 332 |     ckpt_name = _ALLOWED_CHECKPOINT_ALIASES.get(selection, selection)
 333 |     if "/" in ckpt_name or "\\" in ckpt_name or not ckpt_name.endswith(".ckpt"):
 334 |         raise CandidateValidationError("checkpoint_selection must be an allowed alias or checkpoint filename")
 335 |     ckpt_file = ckpt_root / ckpt_name
 336 |     ae_file = ckpt_root / "complexa_ae.ckpt"
 337 |     return ckpt_root, ckpt_name, ae_file
 338 | 
 339 | 
 340 | def _hydra_list(values: list[Any]) -> str:
 341 |     return json.dumps(values, separators=(",", ":"))
 342 | 
 343 | 
 344 | def _build_overrides(spec: dict[str, Any], root_path: Path) -> list[str]:
 345 |     ckpt_root, ckpt_name, ae_file = _resolve_checkpoint(spec)
 346 |     sampling = spec["sampling"]
 347 |     search = spec["search"]
 348 |     computed_max_batch = max(
 349 |         spec["batch_size"],
 350 |         spec["batch_size"] * spec["num_length_samples"],
 351 |         spec["batch_size"] * spec["num_length_samples"] * search["best_of_n"]["replicas"],
 352 |         spec["batch_size"]
 353 |         * search["beam_search"]["n_branch"]
 354 |         * search["beam_search"]["beam_width"],
 355 |     )
 356 |     # Cap peak GPU memory on consumer GPUs (e.g. 24 GB).  When max_batch_size is
 357 |     # too large, BestOfN skips chunking and runs the full expanded batch at once.
 358 |     max_batch_cap = _as_int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_MAX_BATCH_SIZE", 4), "max_batch_cap", 1, 32)
 359 |     max_batch_size = min(computed_max_batch, max_batch_cap)
 360 | 
 361 |     return [
 362 |         f"++root_path={root_path}",
 363 |         "++run_name=skydiscover_3di3_il7ra",
 364 |         "++gen_njobs=1",
 365 |         f"++seed={spec['seed']}",
 366 |         f"++ckpt_path={ckpt_root}",
 367 |         f"++ckpt_name={ckpt_name}",
 368 |         f"++autoencoder_ckpt_path={ae_file}",
 369 |         f"++generation.task_name={TARGET_NAME}",
 370 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.source=skydiscover",
 371 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.target_filename=3di3_chain_b_il7ra_target",
 372 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.target_path={TARGET_PDB_PATH}",
 373 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.target_input={TARGET_METADATA['target']['proteina_target_input']}",
 374 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.hotspot_residues={_hydra_list(spec['hotspot_residues'])}",
 375 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.binder_length={_hydra_list(spec['binder_length'])}",
 376 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.pdb_id=3di3",
 377 |         f"++generation.dataloader.batch_size={spec['batch_size']}",
 378 |         f"++generation.dataloader.dataset.nres.nsamples={spec['num_length_samples']}",
 379 |         f"++generation.args.nsteps={spec['denoising_steps']}",
 380 |         f"++generation.args.self_cond={str(spec['self_conditioning']).lower()}",
 381 |         f"++generation.search.algorithm={search['algorithm']}",
 382 |         f"++generation.search.max_batch_size={max_batch_size}",
 383 |         f"++generation.search.step_checkpoints={_hydra_list([0, spec['denoising_steps']])}",
 384 |         f"++generation.search.best_of_n.replicas={search['best_of_n']['replicas']}",
 385 |         f"++generation.search.beam_search.n_branch={search['beam_search']['n_branch']}",
 386 |         f"++generation.search.beam_search.beam_width={search['beam_search']['beam_width']}",
 387 |         f"++generation.search.fk_steering.n_branch={search['fk_steering']['n_branch']}",
 388 |         f"++generation.search.fk_steering.beam_width={search['fk_steering']['beam_width']}",
 389 |         f"++generation.search.fk_steering.temperature={search['fk_steering']['temperature']}",
 390 |         f"++generation.search.mcts.n_simulations={search['mcts']['n_simulations']}",
 391 |         f"++generation.search.mcts.exploration_prob={search['mcts']['exploration_prob']}",
 392 |         f"++generation.search.mcts.exploration_constant={search['mcts']['exploration_constant']}",
 393 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.schedule.mode={sampling['bb_ca_schedule']['mode']}",
 394 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.schedule.p={sampling['bb_ca_schedule']['p']}",
 395 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.schedule.mode={sampling['local_latents_schedule']['mode']}",
 396 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.schedule.p={sampling['local_latents_schedule']['p']}",
 397 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.gt.mode={sampling['bb_ca_noise']['mode']}",
 398 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.gt.p={sampling['bb_ca_noise']['p']}",
 399 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.gt.mode={sampling['local_latents_noise']['mode']}",
 400 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.gt.p={sampling['local_latents_noise']['p']}",
 401 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.simulation_step_params.sc_scale_noise={sampling['bb_ca_sc_scale_noise']}",
 402 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.simulation_step_params.sc_scale_noise={sampling['local_latents_sc_scale_noise']}",
 403 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.simulation_step_params.sc_scale_score={sampling['bb_ca_sc_scale_score']}",
 404 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.simulation_step_params.sc_scale_score={sampling['local_latents_sc_scale_score']}",
 405 |     ]

 407 | 
 408 | def _check_runtime_requirements(spec: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
 409 |     if not PROTEINA_ROOT.exists():
 410 |         raise RuntimeError(f"Proteina-Complexa repo not found: {PROTEINA_ROOT}")
 411 |     if not (PROTEINA_ROOT / "configs" / f"{PROTEINA_CONFIG_NAME}.yaml").exists():
 412 |         raise RuntimeError(f"Proteina config not found: {PROTEINA_CONFIG_NAME}")
 413 |     if not TARGET_PDB_PATH.exists():
 414 |         raise RuntimeError(f"target PDB not found: {TARGET_PDB_PATH}")
 415 | 
 416 |     ckpt_root, ckpt_name, ae_file = _resolve_checkpoint(spec)
 417 |     ckpt_file = ckpt_root / ckpt_name
 418 |     missing = []
 419 |     if not ckpt_file.exists():
 420 |         missing.append(str(ckpt_file))
 421 |     if not ae_file.exists():
 422 |         missing.append(str(ae_file))
 423 |     af2_dir = os.environ.get("AF2_DIR")
 424 |     if not af2_dir or not Path(af2_dir).exists():
 425 |         missing.append("AF2_DIR")
 426 |     if missing:
 427 |         raise RuntimeError(
 428 |             "missing Proteina runtime assets: "
 429 |             + ", ".join(missing)
 430 |             + ". Set CKPT_PATH and AF2_DIR, or run with SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_VALIDATE_ONLY=1 for schema checks."
 431 |         )
 432 | 
 433 | 
 434 | def _run_proteina_generate(spec: dict[str, Any], *, stage: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 435 |     if os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_VALIDATE_ONLY") == "1":
 436 |         return {
 437 |             "combined_score": 0.0,
 438 |             "validation_only": 1.0,
 439 |             "num_valid_designs": 0,
 440 |             "best_total_reward": 0.0,
 441 |             "mean_total_reward": 0.0,
 442 |             "selected_hotspots": ",".join(spec["hotspot_residues"]),
 443 |             "stage": stage,
 444 |         }
 445 | 
 446 |     _check_runtime_requirements(spec)
 447 |     timeout = int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_TIMEOUT", DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS))
 448 | 
 449 |     with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory(prefix=f"skydiscover_binder_{stage}_") as tmp:
 450 |         root_path = Path(tmp) / "generation"
 451 |         root_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 452 |         cmd = [
 453 |             str(PROTEINA_PYTHON),
 454 |             "-m",
 455 |             "proteinfoundation.generate",
 456 |             "--config-path",
 457 |             str(PROTEINA_CONFIG_DIR),
 458 |             "--config-name",
 459 |             PROTEINA_CONFIG_NAME,
 460 |             *_build_overrides(spec, root_path),
 461 |         ]
 462 |         env = os.environ.copy()
 463 |         env["HYDRA_FULL_ERROR"] = "1"
 464 |         env.setdefault("PYTORCH_CUDA_ALLOC_CONF", "expandable_segments:True")
 465 |         env.setdefault("CUDA_DEVICE_ORDER", "PCI_BUS_ID")
 466 |         src_path = str(PROTEINA_ROOT / "src")
 467 |         env["PYTHONPATH"] = src_path + (os.pathsep + env["PYTHONPATH"] if env.get("PYTHONPATH") else "")
 468 | 
 469 |         start = time.time()
 470 |         proc = subprocess.run(
 471 |             cmd,
 472 |             cwd=str(PROTEINA_ROOT),
 473 |             env=env,
 474 |             text=True,
 475 |             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
 476 |             stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
 477 |             timeout=timeout,
 478 |             check=False,
 479 |         )
 480 |         elapsed = time.time() - start
 481 |         if proc.returncode != 0:
 482 |             raise RuntimeError(
 483 |                 f"Proteina generation failed with exit code {proc.returncode}\n"
 484 |                 f"STDOUT:\n{proc.stdout[-4000:]}\nSTDERR:\n{proc.stderr[-4000:]}"
 485 |             )
 486 |         reward_csvs = sorted(root_path.rglob("rewards_*.csv"))
 487 |         if not reward_csvs:
 488 |             raise RuntimeError(f"Proteina generation completed but no rewards_*.csv found under {root_path}")
 489 |         return _score_reward_csv(reward_csvs[-1], spec=spec, elapsed=elapsed, stage=stage)
 490 | 
 491 | 
 492 | def _finite_float(value: str | None) -> float | None:
 493 |     if value is None or value == "":
 494 |         return None
 495 |     try:
 496 |         parsed = float(value)
 497 |     except ValueError:
 498 |         return None
 499 |     return parsed if math.isfinite(parsed) else None
 500 | 
 501 | 
 502 | def _score_reward_csv(csv_path: Path, *, spec: dict[str, Any], elapsed: float, stage: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 503 |     rows: list[dict[str, str]] = []
 504 |     with csv_path.open(newline="") as f:
 505 |         reader = csv.DictReader(f)
 506 |         rows.extend(reader)
 507 |     reward_rows = [(row, _finite_float(row.get("total_reward"))) for row in rows]
 508 |     reward_rows = [(row, reward) for row, reward in reward_rows if reward is not None]
 509 |     if not reward_rows:
 510 |         raise RuntimeError(f"no finite total_reward values found in {csv_path}")
 511 | 
 512 |     rewards = [reward for _, reward in reward_rows]
 513 |     best_row, best_reward = max(reward_rows, key=lambda item: item[1])
 514 |     mean_reward = sum(rewards) / len(rewards)
 515 |     # Proteina's default AF2 binder reward is often negative interface PAE loss.
 516 |     # Convert it to a bounded higher-is-better score while preserving ranking.
 517 |     penalty = max(0.0, -best_reward)
 518 |     combined = 1.0 / (1.0 + penalty)
 519 |     diversity_bonus = min(len({row.get("aatype", "") for row, _ in reward_rows}), 10) / 100.0
 520 |     combined_score = min(1.0, combined + diversity_bonus)
 521 | 
 522 |     numeric_components: dict[str, float] = {}
 523 |     for key in best_row:
 524 |         if key in {"pdb_path", "aatype", "sample_type", "metadata_tag"}:
 525 |             continue
 526 |         value = _finite_float(best_row.get(key))
 527 |         if value is not None:
 528 |             numeric_components[f"best_{key}"] = value
 529 | 
 530 |     return {
 531 |         "combined_score": float(combined_score),
 532 |         "best_total_reward": float(best_reward),
 533 |         "mean_total_reward": float(mean_reward),
 534 |         "num_valid_designs": float(len(reward_rows)),
 535 |         "eval_time": float(elapsed),
 536 |         "stage": stage,
 537 |         "selected_hotspot_count": float(len(spec["hotspot_residues"])),
 538 |         "binder_min_len": float(spec["binder_length"][0]),
 539 |         "binder_max_len": float(spec["binder_length"][1]),
 540 |         "denoising_steps": float(spec["denoising_steps"]),
 541 |         "selected_hotspots": ",".join(spec["hotspot_residues"]),
 542 |         "search_algorithm": spec["search"]["algorithm"],
 543 |         "reward_csv": str(csv_path),
 544 |         **numeric_components,
 545 |     }
 546 | 
 547 | 
 548 | def _failure(exc: Exception, *, stage: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 549 |     return {
 550 |         "combined_score": 0.0,
 551 |         "best_total_reward": float("nan"),
 552 |         "mean_total_reward": float("nan"),
 553 |         "num_valid_designs": 0.0,
 554 |         "stage": stage,
 555 |         "error": str(exc),
 556 |     }
 557 | 
 558 | 
 559 | def _evaluate(program_path: str, *, stage: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 560 |     try:
 561 |         raw_spec = _load_candidate_spec(program_path)
 562 |         spec = _normalise_spec(raw_spec, stage=stage)
 563 |         result = _run_proteina_generate(spec, stage=stage)
 564 |         result["spec_json"] = json.dumps(spec, sort_keys=True)
 565 |         print(
 566 |             "Evaluation: "
 567 |             f"stage={stage}, combined_score={result['combined_score']:.6f}, "
 568 |             f"best_total_reward={result['best_total_reward']}, "
 569 |             f"hotspots={result.get('selected_hotspots', '')}"
 570 |         )
 571 |         return result
 572 |     except Exception as exc:
 573 |         print(f"Evaluation failed: {exc}")
 574 |         traceback.print_exc()
 575 |         return _failure(exc, stage=stage)
 576 | 
 577 | 
 578 | def evaluate_stage1(program_path: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 579 |     """Fast cascade stage for schema validation and a tiny Proteina run."""
 580 |     return _evaluate(program_path, stage="stage1")
 581 | 
 582 | 
 583 | def evaluate_stage2(program_path: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 584 |     """Full benchmark stage for promising candidates."""
 585 |     return _evaluate(program_path, stage="stage2")
 586 | 
 587 | 
 588 | def evaluate(program_path: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 589 |     """Evaluate one evolved Proteina binder-design run specification."""
 590 |     return evaluate_stage2(program_path)
 591 | 
 592 | 
 593 | if __name__ == "__main__":
 594 |     default_program = BENCHMARK_DIR / "initial_program.py"
 595 |     candidate = sys.argv[1] if len(sys.argv) > 1 else str(default_program)
 596 |     print(json.dumps(evaluate(candidate), indent=2, sort_keys=True))

  28 | 
  29 |     ## Task
  30 |     Improve the EVOLVE-BLOCK in `initial_program.py`. The evolved program must
  31 |     return a Python dictionary from `propose_design_run()` (or `run_discovery()`)
  32 |     describing one bounded Proteina-Complexa run. Do not run Proteina yourself,
  33 |     import external libraries, access the filesystem, spawn subprocesses, or
  34 |     fabricate metrics. The evaluator validates your dictionary and performs the
  35 |     actual model run.
  36 | 
  37 |     ## Target
  38 |     The target is RCSB PDB 3DI3 chain B: human IL-7 receptor alpha ectodomain.
  39 |     The benchmark-local target PDB is a cleaned chain-B-only structure with 193
  40 |     modeled residues. Proteina uses hotspot strings of the form `B84`.
  41 | 
  42 |     Prior art from the RFdiffusion/OpenProtein IL-7Ralpha tutorial uses original
  43 |     chain-B positions `B62`, `B84`, and `B143`. Treat them as a strong baseline,
  44 |     not a hard rule. You may choose other modeled chain-B hotspot residues if
  45 |     your reasoning suggests a better epitope.
  46 | 
  47 |     Contact-derived interface hotspot candidates from the downloaded 3DI3
  48 |     IL-7/IL-7Ralpha complex include:
  49 |       B77, B192, B31, B193, B138, B80, B139, B82, B81, B79,
  50 |       B57, B58, B83, B78, B59, B33, B191, B102, B104
  51 | 
  52 |     ## Candidate Schema
  53 |     Return a dict with these keys. Keep values in the supported ranges.
  54 | 
  55 |     - `hotspot_residues`: 1 to 8 modeled chain-B residues, e.g. `["B62", "B84", "B143"]`.
  56 |     - `binder_length`: `[min_len, max_len]`, each 40 to 220, with min <= max and range width <= 120.
  57 |     - `checkpoint_selection`: use `"complexa_default"` unless you know another checkpoint filename exists under `CKPT_PATH`.
  58 |     - `denoising_steps`: 10 to 400. Larger can improve samples but costs more; cascade evaluation caps this for early stages.
  59 |     - `self_conditioning`: boolean.
  60 |     - `seed`: non-negative integer.
  61 |     - `num_length_samples`: 1 to 8. On 24 GB GPUs the evaluator caps stage 2 to 2.
  62 |     - `batch_size`: 1 to 8. On 24 GB GPUs the evaluator caps stage 2 to 2.
  63 |     - `sampling`: dict with:
  64 |       - `bb_ca_schedule`, `local_latents_schedule`: `{"mode": "log"|"power"|"uniform", "p": 0.05..8.0}`
  65 |       - `bb_ca_noise`, `local_latents_noise`: `{"mode": "1/t"|"tan"|"1-t/t"|"1/t2"|"1/t1p5"|"2/t"|"2/t2"|"2/t1p5", "p": 0.05..8.0}`
  66 |         (do **not** use `power`, `log`, or `linear` for noise — Proteina will crash)
  67 |       - `bb_ca_sc_scale_noise`, `local_latents_sc_scale_noise`: 0.0..2.0
  68 |       - `bb_ca_sc_scale_score`, `local_latents_sc_scale_score`: 0.0..5.0
  69 |     - `search`: dict with:
  70 |       - `algorithm`: one of `single-pass`, `best-of-n`, `beam-search`, `fk-steering`, `mcts`

  72 |       - `beam_search.n_branch`, `beam_search.beam_width`: 1..8

  74 |       - `fk_steering.temperature`: 0.0..5.0

  76 |       - `mcts.exploration_prob`: 0.0..1.0
  77 |       - `mcts.exploration_constant`: 0.0..10.0
  78 | 
  79 |     ## Objective
  80 |     Maximize the evaluator's `combined_score`. The evaluator runs Proteina's
  81 |     binder generation pipeline against 3DI3 chain B and reads Proteina's own
  82 |     `rewards_*.csv`. The primary signal is `total_reward`, which is driven by
  83 |     Proteina's configured binder reward model. Higher is better.
  84 | 
  85 |     Good candidates should make a focused epitope choice, keep runtime bounded,
  86 |     and choose search/test-time-scaling settings that improve the chance of a
  87 |     strong binder without exploding the evaluation cost.
  88 | 
  89 |     ## Constraints
  90 |     - Keep the program pure Python with no imports except `from __future__` and `typing`.
  91 |     - Do not use file I/O, subprocesses, network calls, eval/exec, or dynamic imports.
  92 |     - Do not return multiple candidate specs or implement a local search loop.
  93 |     - The evaluator will reject invalid residue IDs, unsupported algorithms,
  94 |       impossible length ranges, unsafe source code, or missing entry points.
  95 |     - **24 GB GPU memory limits (enforced in evaluator):** stage 2 caps

  97 |       and `max_batch_size` to 4 so Proteina chunks BestOfN batches. Prefer
  98 |       `batch_size=2`, `num_length_samples=2`, `best_of_n.replicas=2` — do not

  61 | def _is_module_docstring(node: ast.AST) -> bool:
  62 |     return isinstance(node, ast.Expr) and isinstance(node.value, ast.Constant) and isinstance(node.value.value, str)
  63 | 
  64 | 
  65 | def _is_main_guard(node: ast.AST) -> bool:
  66 |     if not isinstance(node, ast.If) or node.orelse:
  67 |         return False
  68 |     test = node.test
  69 |     if not isinstance(test, ast.Compare) or len(test.ops) != 1 or len(test.comparators) != 1:
  70 |         return False
  71 |     return (
  72 |         isinstance(test.left, ast.Name)
  73 |         and test.left.id == "__name__"
  74 |         and isinstance(test.ops[0], ast.Eq)
  75 |         and isinstance(test.comparators[0], ast.Constant)
  76 |         and test.comparators[0].value == "__main__"
  77 |     )

  80 | def _validate_candidate_source(program_path: str) -> None:
  81 |     source = Path(program_path).read_text()
  82 |     tree = ast.parse(source, filename=program_path)
  83 |     has_entrypoint = False
  84 | 
  85 |     for node in tree.body:
  86 |         if _is_module_docstring(node) or _is_main_guard(node):
  87 |             continue
  88 |         if isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):
  89 |             if node.module not in _ALLOWED_IMPORT_MODULES:
  90 |                 raise CandidateValidationError(f"import from {node.module!r} is not allowed")
  91 |             continue
  92 |         if isinstance(node, ast.Assign):
  93 |             try:
  94 |                 ast.literal_eval(node.value)
  95 |             except Exception as exc:
  96 |                 raise CandidateValidationError("top-level assignments must be literal constants") from exc
  97 |             continue
  98 |         if isinstance(node, ast.FunctionDef):
  99 |             if node.decorator_list:
 100 |                 raise CandidateValidationError("function decorators are not allowed")
 101 |             if node.name in {"propose_design_run", "run_discovery"}:
 102 |                 has_entrypoint = True
 103 |             for child in ast.walk(node):
 104 |                 if isinstance(child, (ast.Import, ast.ImportFrom)):
 105 |                     raise CandidateValidationError("imports inside evolved functions are not allowed")
 106 |                 if isinstance(child, ast.Call) and isinstance(child.func, ast.Name) and child.func.id in _FORBIDDEN_CALLS:
 107 |                     raise CandidateValidationError(f"call to {child.func.id}() is not allowed")
 108 |             continue
 109 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"top-level {type(node).__name__} is not allowed")
 110 | 
 111 |     if not has_entrypoint:
 112 |         raise CandidateValidationError("candidate must define propose_design_run() or run_discovery()")

 115 | def _load_candidate_spec(program_path: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 116 |     _validate_candidate_source(program_path)
 117 |     spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("binder_candidate", program_path)
 118 |     if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
 119 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"could not load candidate: {program_path}")
 120 |     module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
 121 |     spec.loader.exec_module(module)
 122 | 
 123 |     fn = getattr(module, "propose_design_run", None) or getattr(module, "run_discovery", None)
 124 |     if fn is None:
 125 |         raise CandidateValidationError("missing propose_design_run() or run_discovery()")
 126 |     result = fn()
 127 |     if not isinstance(result, dict):
 128 |         raise CandidateValidationError("candidate entry point must return a dict")
 129 |     return result

 132 | def _as_int(value: Any, name: str, low: int, high: int) -> int:
 133 |     if isinstance(value, bool):
 134 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be an integer")
 135 |     try:
 136 |         out = int(value)
 137 |     except Exception as exc:
 138 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be an integer") from exc
 139 |     if out < low or out > high:
 140 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be between {low} and {high}")
 141 |     return out
 142 |

 144 | def _as_float(value: Any, name: str, low: float, high: float) -> float:
 145 |     try:
 146 |         out = float(value)
 147 |     except Exception as exc:
 148 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be a number") from exc
 149 |     if not math.isfinite(out) or out < low or out > high:
 150 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be finite and between {low} and {high}")
 151 |     return out

 154 | def _normalise_hotspots(value: Any) -> list[str]:
 155 |     if value is None:
 156 |         value = PRIOR_HOTSPOTS
 157 |     if not isinstance(value, (list, tuple)):
 158 |         raise CandidateValidationError("hotspot_residues must be a list")
 159 |     hotspots = []
 160 |     for item in value:
 161 |         if not isinstance(item, str):
 162 |             raise CandidateValidationError("hotspot residues must be strings like 'B84'")
 163 |         residue = item.strip().upper()
 164 |         if not re.fullmatch(r"B\d+[A-Z]?", residue):
 165 |             raise CandidateValidationError(f"invalid hotspot residue format: {item!r}")
 166 |         if residue not in ALLOWED_HOTSPOTS:
 167 |             raise CandidateValidationError(f"hotspot {residue!r} is not a modeled chain-B residue")
 168 |         if residue not in hotspots:
 169 |             hotspots.append(residue)
 170 |     if not 1 <= len(hotspots) <= 8:
 171 |         raise CandidateValidationError("choose between 1 and 8 hotspot residues")
 172 |     return hotspots

 175 | def _normalise_length_range(value: Any) -> list[int]:
 176 |     if not isinstance(value, (list, tuple)) or len(value) != 2:
 177 |         raise CandidateValidationError("binder_length must be [min_len, max_len]")
 178 |     low = _as_int(value[0], "binder_length[0]", 40, 220)
 179 |     high = _as_int(value[1], "binder_length[1]", 40, 220)
 180 |     if low > high:
 181 |         raise CandidateValidationError("binder_length minimum cannot exceed maximum")
 182 |     if high - low > 120:
 183 |         raise CandidateValidationError("binder_length range is too wide for this benchmark")
 184 |     return [low, high]

 188 |     if value is None:

 195 |     return {"mode": mode, "p": _as_float(value.get("p", 1.0), f"{name}.p", 0.05, 8.0)}

 329 | def _resolve_checkpoint(spec: dict[str, Any]) -> tuple[Path, str, Path]:
 330 |     ckpt_root = Path(os.environ.get("CKPT_PATH", str(PROTEINA_ROOT / "ckpts"))).expanduser()
 331 |     selection = spec["checkpoint_selection"]
 332 |     ckpt_name = _ALLOWED_CHECKPOINT_ALIASES.get(selection, selection)
 333 |     if "/" in ckpt_name or "\\" in ckpt_name or not ckpt_name.endswith(".ckpt"):
 334 |         raise CandidateValidationError("checkpoint_selection must be an allowed alias or checkpoint filename")
 335 |     ckpt_file = ckpt_root / ckpt_name
 336 |     ae_file = ckpt_root / "complexa_ae.ckpt"
 337 |     return ckpt_root, ckpt_name, ae_file

 340 | def _hydra_list(values: list[Any]) -> str:
 341 |     return json.dumps(values, separators=(",", ":"))

 344 | def _build_overrides(spec: dict[str, Any], root_path: Path) -> list[str]:
 345 |     ckpt_root, ckpt_name, ae_file = _resolve_checkpoint(spec)
 346 |     sampling = spec["sampling"]
 347 |     search = spec["search"]
 348 |     computed_max_batch = max(
 349 |         spec["batch_size"],
 350 |         spec["batch_size"] * spec["num_length_samples"],
 351 |         spec["batch_size"] * spec["num_length_samples"] * search["best_of_n"]["replicas"],
 352 |         spec["batch_size"]
 353 |         * search["beam_search"]["n_branch"]
 354 |         * search["beam_search"]["beam_width"],
 355 |     )
 356 |     # Cap peak GPU memory on consumer GPUs (e.g. 24 GB).  When max_batch_size is
 357 |     # too large, BestOfN skips chunking and runs the full expanded batch at once.
 358 |     max_batch_cap = _as_int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_MAX_BATCH_SIZE", 4), "max_batch_cap", 1, 32)
 359 |     max_batch_size = min(computed_max_batch, max_batch_cap)
 360 | 
 361 |     return [
 362 |         f"++root_path={root_path}",
 363 |         "++run_name=skydiscover_3di3_il7ra",
 364 |         "++gen_njobs=1",
 365 |         f"++seed={spec['seed']}",
 366 |         f"++ckpt_path={ckpt_root}",
 367 |         f"++ckpt_name={ckpt_name}",
 368 |         f"++autoencoder_ckpt_path={ae_file}",
 369 |         f"++generation.task_name={TARGET_NAME}",
 370 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.source=skydiscover",
 371 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.target_filename=3di3_chain_b_il7ra_target",
 372 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.target_path={TARGET_PDB_PATH}",
 373 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.target_input={TARGET_METADATA['target']['proteina_target_input']}",
 374 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.hotspot_residues={_hydra_list(spec['hotspot_residues'])}",
 375 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.binder_length={_hydra_list(spec['binder_length'])}",
 376 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.pdb_id=3di3",
 377 |         f"++generation.dataloader.batch_size={spec['batch_size']}",
 378 |         f"++generation.dataloader.dataset.nres.nsamples={spec['num_length_samples']}",
 379 |         f"++generation.args.nsteps={spec['denoising_steps']}",
 380 |         f"++generation.args.self_cond={str(spec['self_conditioning']).lower()}",
 381 |         f"++generation.search.algorithm={search['algorithm']}",
 382 |         f"++generation.search.max_batch_size={max_batch_size}",
 383 |         f"++generation.search.step_checkpoints={_hydra_list([0, spec['denoising_steps']])}",
 384 |         f"++generation.search.best_of_n.replicas={search['best_of_n']['replicas']}",
 385 |         f"++generation.search.beam_search.n_branch={search['beam_search']['n_branch']}",
 386 |         f"++generation.search.beam_search.beam_width={search['beam_search']['beam_width']}",
 387 |         f"++generation.search.fk_steering.n_branch={search['fk_steering']['n_branch']}",
 388 |         f"++generation.search.fk_steering.beam_width={search['fk_steering']['beam_width']}",

 391 |         f"++generation.search.mcts.exploration_prob={search['mcts']['exploration_prob']}",

 405 |     ]
 406 | 
 407 | 
 408 | def _check_runtime_requirements(spec: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
 409 |     if not PROTEINA_ROOT.exists():
 410 |         raise RuntimeError(f"Proteina-Complexa repo not found: {PROTEINA_ROOT}")
 411 |     if not (PROTEINA_ROOT / "configs" / f"{PROTEINA_CONFIG_NAME}.yaml").exists():
 412 |         raise RuntimeError(f"Proteina config not found: {PROTEINA_CONFIG_NAME}")
 413 |     if not TARGET_PDB_PATH.exists():
 414 |         raise RuntimeError(f"target PDB not found: {TARGET_PDB_PATH}")
 415 | 
 416 |     ckpt_root, ckpt_name, ae_file = _resolve_checkpoint(spec)
 417 |     ckpt_file = ckpt_root / ckpt_name
 418 |     missing = []
 419 |     if not ckpt_file.exists():
 420 |         missing.append(str(ckpt_file))
 421 |     if not ae_file.exists():
 422 |         missing.append(str(ae_file))
 423 |     af2_dir = os.environ.get("AF2_DIR")
 424 |     if not af2_dir or not Path(af2_dir).exists():
 425 |         missing.append("AF2_DIR")
 426 |     if missing:
 427 |         raise RuntimeError(
 428 |             "missing Proteina runtime assets: "
 429 |             + ", ".join(missing)
 430 |             + ". Set CKPT_PATH and AF2_DIR, or run with SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_VALIDATE_ONLY=1 for schema checks."
 431 |         )
 432 | 
 433 | 
 434 | def _run_proteina_generate(spec: dict[str, Any], *, stage: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 435 |     if os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_VALIDATE_ONLY") == "1":
 436 |         return {
 437 |             "combined_score": 0.0,
 438 |             "validation_only": 1.0,
 439 |             "num_valid_designs": 0,
 440 |             "best_total_reward": 0.0,
 441 |             "mean_total_reward": 0.0,
 442 |             "selected_hotspots": ",".join(spec["hotspot_residues"]),
 443 |             "stage": stage,
 444 |         }
 445 | 
 446 |     _check_runtime_requirements(spec)
 447 |     timeout = int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_TIMEOUT", DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS))
 448 | 
 449 |     with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory(prefix=f"skydiscover_binder_{stage}_") as tmp:
 450 |         root_path = Path(tmp) / "generation"
 451 |         root_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 452 |         cmd = [
 453 |             str(PROTEINA_PYTHON),
 454 |             "-m",
 455 |             "proteinfoundation.generate",
 456 |             "--config-path",
 457 |             str(PROTEINA_CONFIG_DIR),
 458 |             "--config-name",
 459 |             PROTEINA_CONFIG_NAME,
 460 |             *_build_overrides(spec, root_path),
 461 |         ]
 462 |         env = os.environ.copy()
 463 |         env["HYDRA_FULL_ERROR"] = "1"
 464 |         env.setdefault("PYTORCH_CUDA_ALLOC_CONF", "expandable_segments:True")
 465 |         env.setdefault("CUDA_DEVICE_ORDER", "PCI_BUS_ID")
 466 |         src_path = str(PROTEINA_ROOT / "src")
 467 |         env["PYTHONPATH"] = src_path + (os.pathsep + env["PYTHONPATH"] if env.get("PYTHONPATH") else "")
 468 | 
 469 |         start = time.time()
 470 |         proc = subprocess.run(
 471 |             cmd,
 472 |             cwd=str(PROTEINA_ROOT),
 473 |             env=env,
 474 |             text=True,
 475 |             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
 476 |             stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
 477 |             timeout=timeout,
 478 |             check=False,
 479 |         )
 480 |         elapsed = time.time() - start
 481 |         if proc.returncode != 0:
 482 |             raise RuntimeError(
 483 |                 f"Proteina generation failed with exit code {proc.returncode}\n"
 484 |                 f"STDOUT:\n{proc.stdout[-4000:]}\nSTDERR:\n{proc.stderr[-4000:]}"
 485 |             )
 486 |         reward_csvs = sorted(root_path.rglob("rewards_*.csv"))
 487 |         if not reward_csvs:
 488 |             raise RuntimeError(f"Proteina generation completed but no rewards_*.csv found under {root_path}")
 489 |         return _score_reward_csv(reward_csvs[-1], spec=spec, elapsed=elapsed, stage=stage)
 490 | 
 491 | 
 492 | def _finite_float(value: str | None) -> float | None:
 493 |     if value is None or value == "":
 494 |         return None
 495 |     try:
 496 |         parsed = float(value)
 497 |     except ValueError:
 498 |         return None
 499 |     return parsed if math.isfinite(parsed) else None
 500 | 
 501 | 
 502 | def _score_reward_csv(csv_path: Path, *, spec: dict[str, Any], elapsed: float, stage: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 503 |     rows: list[dict[str, str]] = []
 504 |     with csv_path.open(newline="") as f:
 505 |         reader = csv.DictReader(f)
 506 |         rows.extend(reader)
 507 |     reward_rows = [(row, _finite_float(row.get("total_reward"))) for row in rows]
 508 |     reward_rows = [(row, reward) for row, reward in reward_rows if reward is not None]
 509 |     if not reward_rows:
 510 |         raise RuntimeError(f"no finite total_reward values found in {csv_path}")
 511 | 
 512 |     rewards = [reward for _, reward in reward_rows]
 513 |     best_row, best_reward = max(reward_rows, key=lambda item: item[1])
 514 |     mean_reward = sum(rewards) / len(rewards)
 515 |     # Proteina's default AF2 binder reward is often negative interface PAE loss.
 516 |     # Convert it to a bounded higher-is-better score while preserving ranking.
 517 |     penalty = max(0.0, -best_reward)
 518 |     combined = 1.0 / (1.0 + penalty)
 519 |     diversity_bonus = min(len({row.get("aatype", "") for row, _ in reward_rows}), 10) / 100.0
 520 |     combined_score = min(1.0, combined + diversity_bonus)
 521 | 
 522 |     numeric_components: dict[str, float] = {}
 523 |     for key in best_row:
 524 |         if key in {"pdb_path", "aatype", "sample_type", "metadata_tag"}:
 525 |             continue
 526 |         value = _finite_float(best_row.get(key))
 527 |         if value is not None:
 528 |             numeric_components[f"best_{key}"] = value
 529 | 
 530 |     return {
 531 |         "combined_score": float(combined_score),
 532 |         "best_total_reward": float(best_reward),
 533 |         "mean_total_reward": float(mean_reward),
 534 |         "num_valid_designs": float(len(reward_rows)),
 535 |         "eval_time": float(elapsed),
 536 |         "stage": stage,
 537 |         "selected_hotspot_count": float(len(spec["hotspot_residues"])),
 538 |         "binder_min_len": float(spec["binder_length"][0]),
 539 |         "binder_max_len": float(spec["binder_length"][1]),
 540 |         "denoising_steps": float(spec["denoising_steps"]),
 541 |         "selected_hotspots": ",".join(spec["hotspot_residues"]),
 542 |         "search_algorithm": spec["search"]["algorithm"],
 543 |         "reward_csv": str(csv_path),
 544 |         **numeric_components,
 545 |     }
 546 | 
 547 | 
 548 | def _failure(exc: Exception, *, stage: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 549 |     return {
 550 |         "combined_score": 0.0,
 551 |         "best_total_reward": float("nan"),
 552 |         "mean_total_reward": float("nan"),
 553 |         "num_valid_designs": 0.0,
 554 |         "stage": stage,
 555 |         "error": str(exc),
 556 |     }
 557 | 
 558 | 
 559 | def _evaluate(program_path: str, *, stage: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 560 |     try:
 561 |         raw_spec = _load_candidate_spec(program_path)
 562 |         spec = _normalise_spec(raw_spec, stage=stage)
 563 |         result = _run_proteina_generate(spec, stage=stage)
 564 |         result["spec_json"] = json.dumps(spec, sort_keys=True)
 565 |         print(
 566 |             "Evaluation: "
 567 |             f"stage={stage}, combined_score={result['combined_score']:.6f}, "
 568 |             f"best_total_reward={result['best_total_reward']}, "
 569 |             f"hotspots={result.get('selected_hotspots', '')}"
 570 |         )
 571 |         return result
 572 |     except Exception as exc:
 573 |         print(f"Evaluation failed: {exc}")
 574 |         traceback.print_exc()
 575 |         return _failure(exc, stage=stage)
 576 | 
 577 | 
 578 | def evaluate_stage1(program_path: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 579 |     """Fast cascade stage for schema validation and a tiny Proteina run."""
 580 |     return _evaluate(program_path, stage="stage1")
 581 | 
 582 | 
 583 | def evaluate_stage2(program_path: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 584 |     """Full benchmark stage for promising candidates."""
 585 |     return _evaluate(program_path, stage="stage2")
 586 | 
 587 | 
 588 | def evaluate(program_path: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 589 |     """Evaluate one evolved Proteina binder-design run specification."""
 590 |     return evaluate_stage2(program_path)
 591 |

 594 |     default_program = BENCHMARK_DIR / "initial_program.py"
 595 |     candidate = sys.argv[1] if len(sys.argv) > 1 else str(default_program)
 596 |     print(json.dumps(evaluate(candidate), indent=2, sort_keys=True))

  33 | DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 7200
  34 | 
  35 | _FORBIDDEN_CALLS = {"eval", "exec", "compile", "open", "__import__", "input"}
  36 | _ALLOWED_IMPORT_MODULES = {"__future__", "typing"}
  37 | _ALLOWED_SEARCH_ALGORITHMS = {"single-pass", "best-of-n", "beam-search", "fk-steering", "mcts"}
  38 | _ALLOWED_CHECKPOINT_ALIASES = {"complexa_default": "complexa.ckpt", "complexa": "complexa.ckpt"}
  39 | _ALLOWED_SCHEDULE_MODES = {"log", "power", "uniform"}
  40 | # Must match Proteina get_gt() in product_space_flow_matcher.py — not every string
  41 | # in the upstream config docs is implemented.
  42 | _ALLOWED_NOISE_MODES = {"1/t", "tan", "1-t/t", "1/t2", "1/t1p5", "2/t", "2/t2", "2/t1p5"}
  43 | 
  44 | 
  45 | class CandidateValidationError(ValueError):
  46 |     """Raised when an evolved candidate violates the benchmark contract."""
  47 | 
  48 | 
  49 | def _load_metadata() -> dict[str, Any]:
  50 |     with TARGET_METADATA_PATH.open() as f:
  51 |         return json.load(f)
  52 | 
  53 | 
  54 | TARGET_METADATA = _load_metadata()
  55 | ALLOWED_HOTSPOTS = set(TARGET_METADATA["target"]["allowed_hotspots"])
  56 | INTERFACE_HOTSPOTS = [item["hotspot"] for item in TARGET_METADATA["interface_hotspot_candidates"]]
  57 | PRIOR_HOTSPOTS = TARGET_METADATA["prior_art_hotspots"]["hotspots"]
  58 | TARGET_PDB_PATH = ASSETS_DIR / TARGET_METADATA["target"]["target_pdb"]
  59 | 
  60 | 
  61 | def _is_module_docstring(node: ast.AST) -> bool:
  62 |     return isinstance(node, ast.Expr) and isinstance(node.value, ast.Constant) and isinstance(node.value.value, str)
  63 | 
  64 | 
  65 | def _is_main_guard(node: ast.AST) -> bool:
  66 |     if not isinstance(node, ast.If) or node.orelse:
  67 |         return False
  68 |     test = node.test
  69 |     if not isinstance(test, ast.Compare) or len(test.ops) != 1 or len(test.comparators) != 1:
  70 |         return False
  71 |     return (
  72 |         isinstance(test.left, ast.Name)
  73 |         and test.left.id == "__name__"
  74 |         and isinstance(test.ops[0], ast.Eq)
  75 |         and isinstance(test.comparators[0], ast.Constant)
  76 |         and test.comparators[0].value == "__main__"
  77 |     )
  78 | 
  79 | 
  80 | def _validate_candidate_source(program_path: str) -> None:
  81 |     source = Path(program_path).read_text()
  82 |     tree = ast.parse(source, filename=program_path)
  83 |     has_entrypoint = False
  84 | 
  85 |     for node in tree.body:
  86 |         if _is_module_docstring(node) or _is_main_guard(node):
  87 |             continue
  88 |         if isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):
  89 |             if node.module not in _ALLOWED_IMPORT_MODULES:
  90 |                 raise CandidateValidationError(f"import from {node.module!r} is not allowed")
  91 |             continue
  92 |         if isinstance(node, ast.Assign):
  93 |             try:
  94 |                 ast.literal_eval(node.value)
  95 |             except Exception as exc:
  96 |                 raise CandidateValidationError("top-level assignments must be literal constants") from exc
  97 |             continue
  98 |         if isinstance(node, ast.FunctionDef):
  99 |             if node.decorator_list:
 100 |                 raise CandidateValidationError("function decorators are not allowed")
 101 |             if node.name in {"propose_design_run", "run_discovery"}:
 102 |                 has_entrypoint = True
 103 |             for child in ast.walk(node):
 104 |                 if isinstance(child, (ast.Import, ast.ImportFrom)):
 105 |                     raise CandidateValidationError("imports inside evolved functions are not allowed")
 106 |                 if isinstance(child, ast.Call) and isinstance(child.func, ast.Name) and child.func.id in _FORBIDDEN_CALLS:
 107 |                     raise CandidateValidationError(f"call to {child.func.id}() is not allowed")
 108 |             continue
 109 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"top-level {type(node).__name__} is not allowed")
 110 | 
 111 |     if not has_entrypoint:
 112 |         raise CandidateValidationError("candidate must define propose_design_run() or run_discovery()")
 113 | 
 114 | 
 115 | def _load_candidate_spec(program_path: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 116 |     _validate_candidate_source(program_path)
 117 |     spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("binder_candidate", program_path)
 118 |     if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
 119 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"could not load candidate: {program_path}")
 120 |     module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
 121 |     spec.loader.exec_module(module)
 122 | 
 123 |     fn = getattr(module, "propose_design_run", None) or getattr(module, "run_discovery", None)
 124 |     if fn is None:
 125 |         raise CandidateValidationError("missing propose_design_run() or run_discovery()")
 126 |     result = fn()
 127 |     if not isinstance(result, dict):
 128 |         raise CandidateValidationError("candidate entry point must return a dict")
 129 |     return result
 130 | 
 131 | 
 132 | def _as_int(value: Any, name: str, low: int, high: int) -> int:
 133 |     if isinstance(value, bool):
 134 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be an integer")
 135 |     try:
 136 |         out = int(value)
 137 |     except Exception as exc:
 138 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be an integer") from exc
 139 |     if out < low or out > high:
 140 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be between {low} and {high}")
 141 |     return out
 142 | 
 143 | 
 144 | def _as_float(value: Any, name: str, low: float, high: float) -> float:
 145 |     try:
 146 |         out = float(value)
 147 |     except Exception as exc:
 148 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be a number") from exc
 149 |     if not math.isfinite(out) or out < low or out > high:
 150 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be finite and between {low} and {high}")
 151 |     return out
 152 | 
 153 | 
 154 | def _normalise_hotspots(value: Any) -> list[str]:
 155 |     if value is None:
 156 |         value = PRIOR_HOTSPOTS
 157 |     if not isinstance(value, (list, tuple)):
 158 |         raise CandidateValidationError("hotspot_residues must be a list")
 159 |     hotspots = []
 160 |     for item in value:
 161 |         if not isinstance(item, str):
 162 |             raise CandidateValidationError("hotspot residues must be strings like 'B84'")
 163 |         residue = item.strip().upper()
 164 |         if not re.fullmatch(r"B\d+[A-Z]?", residue):
 165 |             raise CandidateValidationError(f"invalid hotspot residue format: {item!r}")
 166 |         if residue not in ALLOWED_HOTSPOTS:
 167 |             raise CandidateValidationError(f"hotspot {residue!r} is not a modeled chain-B residue")
 168 |         if residue not in hotspots:
 169 |             hotspots.append(residue)
 170 |     if not 1 <= len(hotspots) <= 8:
 171 |         raise CandidateValidationError("choose between 1 and 8 hotspot residues")
 172 |     return hotspots
 173 | 
 174 | 
 175 | def _normalise_length_range(value: Any) -> list[int]:
 176 |     if not isinstance(value, (list, tuple)) or len(value) != 2:
 177 |         raise CandidateValidationError("binder_length must be [min_len, max_len]")
 178 |     low = _as_int(value[0], "binder_length[0]", 40, 220)
 179 |     high = _as_int(value[1], "binder_length[1]", 40, 220)
 180 |     if low > high:
 181 |         raise CandidateValidationError("binder_length minimum cannot exceed maximum")
 182 |     if high - low > 120:
 183 |         raise CandidateValidationError("binder_length range is too wide for this benchmark")
 184 |     return [low, high]
 185 | 
 186 | 
 187 | def _normalise_schedule(value: Any, name: str, allowed_modes: set[str]) -> dict[str, Any]:
 188 |     if value is None:
 189 |         value = {}
 190 |     if not isinstance(value, dict):
 191 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name} must be a dict")
 192 |     mode = str(value.get("mode", "log" if "schedule" in name else "1/t"))
 193 |     if mode not in allowed_modes:
 194 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"{name}.mode {mode!r} is unsupported")
 195 |     return {"mode": mode, "p": _as_float(value.get("p", 1.0), f"{name}.p", 0.05, 8.0)}
 196 | 
 197 | 
 198 | def _normalise_spec(raw: dict[str, Any], *, stage: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 199 |     sampling = raw.get("sampling", {})
 200 |     if sampling is None:
 201 |         sampling = {}
 202 |     if not isinstance(sampling, dict):
 203 |         raise CandidateValidationError("sampling must be a dict")
 204 | 
 205 |     search = raw.get("search", {})
 206 |     if search is None:
 207 |         search = {}
 208 |     if not isinstance(search, dict):
 209 |         raise CandidateValidationError("search must be a dict")
 210 | 
 211 |     algorithm = str(search.get("algorithm", "best-of-n"))
 212 |     if algorithm not in _ALLOWED_SEARCH_ALGORITHMS:
 213 |         raise CandidateValidationError(f"unsupported search algorithm: {algorithm!r}")
 214 | 
 215 |     nsteps = _as_int(raw.get("denoising_steps", 80), "denoising_steps", 10, 400)
 216 |     if stage == "stage1":
 217 |         nsteps = min(nsteps, _as_int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_STAGE1_NSTEPS", 20), "stage1_nsteps", 5, 80))
 218 |     else:
 219 |         nsteps = min(nsteps, _as_int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_MAX_NSTEPS", 120), "max_nsteps", 10, 400))
 220 | 
 221 |     stage2_batch_cap = _as_int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_STAGE2_BATCH_SIZE", 2), "stage2_batch_cap", 1, 8)
 222 |     stage2_length_cap = _as_int(
 223 |         os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_STAGE2_NUM_LENGTH_SAMPLES", 2),
 224 |         "stage2_length_cap",
 225 |         1,
 226 |         8,
 227 |     )
 228 |     stage2_replica_cap = _as_int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_STAGE2_REPLICAS", 2), "stage2_replica_cap", 1, 8)
 229 | 
 230 |     batch_size = _as_int(raw.get("batch_size", 2), "batch_size", 1, 8)
 231 |     num_length_samples = _as_int(raw.get("num_length_samples", 2), "num_length_samples", 1, 8)
 232 |     if stage == "stage1":
 233 |         batch_size = min(batch_size, 1)
 234 |         num_length_samples = min(num_length_samples, 1)
 235 |     else:
 236 |         batch_size = min(batch_size, stage2_batch_cap)
 237 |         num_length_samples = min(num_length_samples, stage2_length_cap)
 238 | 
 239 |     best_of_n = search.get("best_of_n", {}) if isinstance(search.get("best_of_n", {}), dict) else {}
 240 |     beam_search = search.get("beam_search", {}) if isinstance(search.get("beam_search", {}), dict) else {}
 241 |     fk_steering = search.get("fk_steering", {}) if isinstance(search.get("fk_steering", {}), dict) else {}
 242 |     mcts = search.get("mcts", {}) if isinstance(search.get("mcts", {}), dict) else {}
 243 | 
 244 |     spec = {
 245 |         "hotspot_residues": _normalise_hotspots(raw.get("hotspot_residues")),
 246 |         "binder_length": _normalise_length_range(raw.get("binder_length", [70, 110])),
 247 |         "checkpoint_selection": str(raw.get("checkpoint_selection", "complexa_default")),
 248 |         "denoising_steps": nsteps,
 249 |         "self_conditioning": bool(raw.get("self_conditioning", True)),
 250 |         "seed": _as_int(raw.get("seed", 7), "seed", 0, 2**31 - 1),
 251 |         "num_length_samples": num_length_samples,
 252 |         "batch_size": batch_size,
 253 |         "sampling": {
 254 |             "bb_ca_schedule": _normalise_schedule(
 255 |                 sampling.get("bb_ca_schedule", {"mode": "log", "p": 2.0}),
 256 |                 "bb_ca_schedule",
 257 |                 _ALLOWED_SCHEDULE_MODES,
 258 |             ),
 259 |             "local_latents_schedule": _normalise_schedule(
 260 |                 sampling.get("local_latents_schedule", {"mode": "power", "p": 2.0}),
 261 |                 "local_latents_schedule",
 262 |                 _ALLOWED_SCHEDULE_MODES,
 263 |             ),
 264 |             "bb_ca_noise": _normalise_schedule(
 265 |                 sampling.get("bb_ca_noise", {"mode": "1/t", "p": 1.0}),
 266 |                 "bb_ca_noise",
 267 |                 _ALLOWED_NOISE_MODES,
 268 |             ),
 269 |             "local_latents_noise": _normalise_schedule(
 270 |                 sampling.get("local_latents_noise", {"mode": "tan", "p": 1.0}),
 271 |                 "local_latents_noise",
 272 |                 _ALLOWED_NOISE_MODES,
 273 |             ),
 274 |             "bb_ca_sc_scale_noise": _as_float(sampling.get("bb_ca_sc_scale_noise", 0.1), "bb_ca_sc_scale_noise", 0.0, 2.0),
 275 |             "local_latents_sc_scale_noise": _as_float(
 276 |                 sampling.get("local_latents_sc_scale_noise", 0.1),
 277 |                 "local_latents_sc_scale_noise",
 278 |                 0.0,
 279 |                 2.0,
 280 |             ),
 281 |             "bb_ca_sc_scale_score": _as_float(sampling.get("bb_ca_sc_scale_score", 1.0), "bb_ca_sc_scale_score", 0.0, 5.0),
 282 |             "local_latents_sc_scale_score": _as_float(
 283 |                 sampling.get("local_latents_sc_scale_score", 1.0),
 284 |                 "local_latents_sc_scale_score",
 285 |                 0.0,
 286 |                 5.0,
 287 |             ),
 288 |         },
 289 |         "search": {
 290 |             "algorithm": algorithm,
 291 |             "best_of_n": {"replicas": _as_int(best_of_n.get("replicas", 2), "best_of_n.replicas", 1, 8)},
 292 |             "beam_search": {
 293 |                 "n_branch": _as_int(beam_search.get("n_branch", 2), "beam_search.n_branch", 1, 8),
 294 |                 "beam_width": _as_int(beam_search.get("beam_width", 2), "beam_search.beam_width", 1, 8),
 295 |             },
 296 |             "fk_steering": {
 297 |                 "n_branch": _as_int(fk_steering.get("n_branch", 2), "fk_steering.n_branch", 1, 8),
 298 |                 "beam_width": _as_int(fk_steering.get("beam_width", 2), "fk_steering.beam_width", 1, 8),
 299 |                 "temperature": _as_float(fk_steering.get("temperature", 0.1), "fk_steering.temperature", 0.0, 5.0),
 300 |             },
 301 |             "mcts": {
 302 |                 "n_simulations": _as_int(mcts.get("n_simulations", 4), "mcts.n_simulations", 1, 64),
 303 |                 "exploration_prob": _as_float(mcts.get("exploration_prob", 0.4), "mcts.exploration_prob", 0.0, 1.0),
 304 |                 "exploration_constant": _as_float(
 305 |                     mcts.get("exploration_constant", 1.0),
 306 |                     "mcts.exploration_constant",
 307 |                     0.0,
 308 |                     10.0,
 309 |                 ),
 310 |             },
 311 |         },
 312 |     }
 313 |     if stage == "stage1":
 314 |         spec["search"]["best_of_n"]["replicas"] = min(spec["search"]["best_of_n"]["replicas"], 1)
 315 |         spec["search"]["beam_search"]["n_branch"] = min(spec["search"]["beam_search"]["n_branch"], 1)
 316 |         spec["search"]["beam_search"]["beam_width"] = min(spec["search"]["beam_search"]["beam_width"], 1)
 317 |         spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["n_branch"] = min(spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["n_branch"], 1)
 318 |         spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["beam_width"] = min(spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["beam_width"], 1)
 319 |         spec["search"]["mcts"]["n_simulations"] = min(spec["search"]["mcts"]["n_simulations"], 2)
 320 |     else:
 321 |         spec["search"]["best_of_n"]["replicas"] = min(spec["search"]["best_of_n"]["replicas"], stage2_replica_cap)
 322 |         spec["search"]["beam_search"]["n_branch"] = min(spec["search"]["beam_search"]["n_branch"], stage2_replica_cap)
 323 |         spec["search"]["beam_search"]["beam_width"] = min(spec["search"]["beam_search"]["beam_width"], stage2_replica_cap)
 324 |         spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["n_branch"] = min(spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["n_branch"], stage2_replica_cap)
 325 |         spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["beam_width"] = min(spec["search"]["fk_steering"]["beam_width"], stage2_replica_cap)
 326 |     return spec

 328 | 
 329 | def _resolve_checkpoint(spec: dict[str, Any]) -> tuple[Path, str, Path]:
 330 |     ckpt_root = Path(os.environ.get("CKPT_PATH", str(PROTEINA_ROOT / "ckpts"))).expanduser()
 331 |     selection = spec["checkpoint_selection"]
 332 |     ckpt_name = _ALLOWED_CHECKPOINT_ALIASES.get(selection, selection)
 333 |     if "/" in ckpt_name or "\\" in ckpt_name or not ckpt_name.endswith(".ckpt"):
 334 |         raise CandidateValidationError("checkpoint_selection must be an allowed alias or checkpoint filename")
 335 |     ckpt_file = ckpt_root / ckpt_name
 336 |     ae_file = ckpt_root / "complexa_ae.ckpt"
 337 |     return ckpt_root, ckpt_name, ae_file
 338 | 
 339 | 
 340 | def _hydra_list(values: list[Any]) -> str:
 341 |     return json.dumps(values, separators=(",", ":"))
 342 | 
 343 | 
 344 | def _build_overrides(spec: dict[str, Any], root_path: Path) -> list[str]:
 345 |     ckpt_root, ckpt_name, ae_file = _resolve_checkpoint(spec)
 346 |     sampling = spec["sampling"]
 347 |     search = spec["search"]
 348 |     computed_max_batch = max(
 349 |         spec["batch_size"],
 350 |         spec["batch_size"] * spec["num_length_samples"],
 351 |         spec["batch_size"] * spec["num_length_samples"] * search["best_of_n"]["replicas"],
 352 |         spec["batch_size"]
 353 |         * search["beam_search"]["n_branch"]
 354 |         * search["beam_search"]["beam_width"],
 355 |     )
 356 |     # Cap peak GPU memory on consumer GPUs (e.g. 24 GB).  When max_batch_size is
 357 |     # too large, BestOfN skips chunking and runs the full expanded batch at once.
 358 |     max_batch_cap = _as_int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_BINDER_MAX_BATCH_SIZE", 4), "max_batch_cap", 1, 32)
 359 |     max_batch_size = min(computed_max_batch, max_batch_cap)
 360 | 
 361 |     return [
 362 |         f"++root_path={root_path}",
 363 |         "++run_name=skydiscover_3di3_il7ra",
 364 |         "++gen_njobs=1",
 365 |         f"++seed={spec['seed']}",
 366 |         f"++ckpt_path={ckpt_root}",
 367 |         f"++ckpt_name={ckpt_name}",
 368 |         f"++autoencoder_ckpt_path={ae_file}",
 369 |         f"++generation.task_name={TARGET_NAME}",
 370 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.source=skydiscover",
 371 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.target_filename=3di3_chain_b_il7ra_target",
 372 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.target_path={TARGET_PDB_PATH}",
 373 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.target_input={TARGET_METADATA['target']['proteina_target_input']}",
 374 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.hotspot_residues={_hydra_list(spec['hotspot_residues'])}",
 375 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.binder_length={_hydra_list(spec['binder_length'])}",
 376 |         f"++generation.target_dict_cfg.{TARGET_NAME}.pdb_id=3di3",
 377 |         f"++generation.dataloader.batch_size={spec['batch_size']}",
 378 |         f"++generation.dataloader.dataset.nres.nsamples={spec['num_length_samples']}",
 379 |         f"++generation.args.nsteps={spec['denoising_steps']}",
 380 |         f"++generation.args.self_cond={str(spec['self_conditioning']).lower()}",
 381 |         f"++generation.search.algorithm={search['algorithm']}",
 382 |         f"++generation.search.max_batch_size={max_batch_size}",
 383 |         f"++generation.search.step_checkpoints={_hydra_list([0, spec['denoising_steps']])}",
 384 |         f"++generation.search.best_of_n.replicas={search['best_of_n']['replicas']}",
 385 |         f"++generation.search.beam_search.n_branch={search['beam_search']['n_branch']}",
 386 |         f"++generation.search.beam_search.beam_width={search['beam_search']['beam_width']}",
 387 |         f"++generation.search.fk_steering.n_branch={search['fk_steering']['n_branch']}",
 388 |         f"++generation.search.fk_steering.beam_width={search['fk_steering']['beam_width']}",
 389 |         f"++generation.search.fk_steering.temperature={search['fk_steering']['temperature']}",
 390 |         f"++generation.search.mcts.n_simulations={search['mcts']['n_simulations']}",
 391 |         f"++generation.search.mcts.exploration_prob={search['mcts']['exploration_prob']}",
 392 |         f"++generation.search.mcts.exploration_constant={search['mcts']['exploration_constant']}",
 393 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.schedule.mode={sampling['bb_ca_schedule']['mode']}",
 394 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.schedule.p={sampling['bb_ca_schedule']['p']}",
 395 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.schedule.mode={sampling['local_latents_schedule']['mode']}",
 396 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.schedule.p={sampling['local_latents_schedule']['p']}",
 397 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.gt.mode={sampling['bb_ca_noise']['mode']}",
 398 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.gt.p={sampling['bb_ca_noise']['p']}",
 399 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.gt.mode={sampling['local_latents_noise']['mode']}",
 400 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.gt.p={sampling['local_latents_noise']['p']}",
 401 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.simulation_step_params.sc_scale_noise={sampling['bb_ca_sc_scale_noise']}",
 402 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.simulation_step_params.sc_scale_noise={sampling['local_latents_sc_scale_noise']}",
 403 |         f"++generation.model.bb_ca.simulation_step_params.sc_scale_score={sampling['bb_ca_sc_scale_score']}",
 404 |         f"++generation.model.local_latents.simulation_step_params.sc_scale_score={sampling['local_latents_sc_scale_score']}",
 405 |     ]
